binwalk

Explicação: Analisa o arquivo em busca de dados comprimidos ou embutidos, comum em firmware ou esteganografia.
DECIMAL       HEXADECIMAL     DESCRIPTION
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
0             0x0             JPEG image data, EXIF standard
12            0xC             TIFF image data, big-endian, offset of first image directory: 8

ent

Explicação: Avalia a aleatoriedade (entropia) do arquivo. Alta entropia pode indicar criptografia ou compactação.
Entropy = 7.922972 bits per byte.

Optimum compression would reduce the size
of this 2623074 byte file by 0 percent.

Chi square distribution for 2623074 samples is 326993.92, and randomly
would exceed this value less than 0.01 percent of the times.

Arithmetic mean value of data bytes is 120.6118 (127.5 = random).
Monte Carlo value for Pi is 3.268528452 (error 4.04 percent).
Serial correlation coefficient is 0.018062 (totally uncorrelated = 0.0).
